Users can RSVP for events, add them to their own calendars, and create reminders.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6 vc_col-lg-4 vc_col-md-4 vc_col-xs-12\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-7164\" src=\"https://storage.googleapis.com/sales.appinst.io/2016/08/brand-control-copy.png\" width=\"146\" height=\"146\" alt=\"add rich media to your app\"></p>\n<h5 style=\"text-align: center;\">Rich Media</h5>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">Boost engagement with your business by adding new content on a regular basis.
